Разными цветами закрашены области притяжения для разных корней. Более тёмные области соответствуют большему числу итераций.</figcaption></figure>
<p>До сих пор в описании метода использовались функции, осуществляющие отображения в пределах <a href="/wiki/%D0%9C%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B6%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%BE" title="Множество">множества</a> <a href="/wiki/%D0%92%D0%B5%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B5_%D1%87%D0%B8%D1%81%D0%BB%D0%BE" title="Вещественное число">вещественных значений</a>. Однако метод может быть применён и для нахождения нуля <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%D0%A4%D1%83%D0%BD%D0%BA%D1%86%D0%B8%D1%8F_%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%BC%D0%BF%D0%BB%D0%B5%D0%BA%D1%81%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B9_%D0%BF%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%BC%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B9" title="Функция комплексной переменной">функции комплексной переменной</a>. При этом процедура остаётся неизменной:
</p>

<p>Особый интерес представляет выбор начального приближения <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z_{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle z_{0}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e72d1d86e86355892b39b8eb32b964834e113bf" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.135ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>. Ввиду того, что функция может иметь несколько нулей, в различных случаях метод может сходиться к различным значениям, и вполне естественно возникает желание выяснить, какие области обеспечат сходимость к тому или иному корню. Этот вопрос заинтересовал <a href="/wiki/%D0%9A%D1%8D%D0%BB%D0%B8,_%D0%90%D1%80%D1%82%D1%83%D1%80" title="Кэли, Артур">Артура Кэли</a> ещё в <a href="/wiki/1879_%D0%B3%D0%BE%D0%B4" title="1879 год">1879 году</a>, однако разрешить его смогли лишь в <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1970-%D0%B5" title="1970-е">70</a>-х годах <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%D0%94%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%B4%D1%86%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%8B%D0%B9_%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BA" title="Двадцатый век">двадцатого столетия</a> с появлением вычислительной техники. Оказалось, что на пересечениях этих областей (их принято называть <i>областями притяжения</i>) образуются так называемые <i><a href="/wiki/%D0%A4%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BA%D1%82%D0%B0%D0%BB" title="Фрактал">фракталы</a></i> — бесконечные самоподобные геометрические фигуры.
</p><p>Ввиду того, что Ньютон применял свой метод исключительно к <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%D0%9F%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%BC" title="Полином">полиномам</a>, фракталы, образованные в результате такого применения, обрели название <i>фракталов Ньютона</i> или <i><a href="/wiki/%D0%91%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%81%D0%B5%D0%B9%D0%BD%D1%8B_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0" title="Бассейны Ньютона">бассейнов Ньютона</a></i>.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span id=".D0.A0.D0.B5.D0.B0.D0.BB.D0.B8.D0.B7.D0.B0.D1.86.D0.B8.D1.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Реализация">Реализация</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=20" title="Редактировать раздел «Реализация»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Редактировать код раздела «Реализация»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Scala">Scala</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=21" title="Редактировать раздел «Scala»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Редактировать код раздела «Scala»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<span class="w">  </span><span class="kd">val</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">accuracy</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">1e-6</span>

<span class="w">  </span><span class="nd">@tailrec</span>
<span class="w">  </span><span class="k">def</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nf">method</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">dfdx</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="p">):</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kd">val</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">/</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">dfdx</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">if</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x1</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">else</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">method</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">dfdx</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="w">  </span><span class="p">}</span>

<span class="w">  </span><span class="k">def</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nf">g</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nc">C</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">Double</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nc">C</span>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Python">Python</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=22" title="Редактировать раздел «Python»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Редактировать код раздела «Python»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-python mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">math</span> <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="n">sin</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">cos</span>
<span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">typing</span> <span class="kn">import</span> <span class="n">Callable</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">unittest</span>


<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">newton</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Callable</span><span class="p">[[</span><span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">f_prime</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Callable</span><span class="p">[[</span><span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">,</span> 
	<span class="n">eps</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mf">1e-7</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">kmax</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mf">1e3</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">:</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="sd">"""</span>
<span class="sd">	solves f(x) = 0 by Newton's method with precision eps</span>
<span class="sd">	:param f: f</span>
<span class="sd">	:param f_prime: f'</span>
<span class="sd">	:param x0: starting point</span>
<span class="sd">	:param eps: precision wanted</span>
<span class="sd">	:return: root of f(x) = 0</span>
<span class="sd">	"""</span>
	<span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">x_prev</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">x0</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">2</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">eps</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
	
	<span class="k">while</span> <span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">x_prev</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">&gt;=</span> <span class="n">eps</span> <span class="ow">and</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="n">kmax</span><span class="p">:</span>
		<span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">x_prev</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">f</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">f_prime</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span>

	<span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">x</span>


<span class="k">class</span> <span class="nc">TestNewton</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">unittest</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">TestCase</span><span class="p">):</span>
	<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">test_0</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
		<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">f</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">:</span>
			<span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">x</span><span class="o">**</span><span class="mi">2</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">20</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">sin</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span>


		<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">f_prime</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">:</span>
			<span class="k">return</span> <span class="mi">2</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">20</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">cos</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span>


		<span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">x_star</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mf">2.7529466338187049383</span>

		<span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">assertAlmostEqual</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">newton</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">f_prime</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">x0</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">x_star</span><span class="p">)</span>


<span class="k">if</span> <span class="vm">__name__</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="s1">'__main__'</span><span class="p">:</span>
	<span class="n">unittest</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">main</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="PHP">PHP</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=23" title="Редактировать раздел «PHP»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Редактировать код раздела «PHP»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-php mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="cp">&lt;?php</span>
<span class="c1">// PHP 5.4</span>
<span class="k">function</span> <span class="nf">newtons_method</span><span class="p">(</span>
	<span class="nv">$a</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nv">$b</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> 
	<span class="nv">$f</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">function</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
	
		<span class="k">return</span> <span class="nb">pow</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$x</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span>
	
	<span class="p">},</span>
	<span class="nv">$derivative_f</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">function</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>

		<span class="k">return</span> <span class="mi">4</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="nb">pow</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$x</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">);</span>
	
	<span class="p">},</span> <span class="nv">$eps</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mf">1E-3</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>

        <span class="nv">$xa</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">$a</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="nv">$xb</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">$b</span><span class="p">;</span>

        <span class="nv">$iteration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span>

        <span class="k">while</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$xb</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="nv">$eps</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>

            <span class="nv">$p1</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">$f</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$xa</span><span class="p">);</span>
            <span class="nv">$q1</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">$derivative_f</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">$xa</span><span class="p">);</span>
            <span class="nv">$xa</span> <span class="o">-=</span> <span class="nv">$p1</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="nv">$q1</span><span class="p">;</span>
            <span class="nv">$xb</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">$p1</span><span class="p">;</span>
            <span class="o">++</span><span class="nv">$iteration</span><span class="p">;</span>

        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nv">$xa</span><span class="p">;</span>

<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Octave">Octave</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=24" title="Редактировать раздел «Octave»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Редактировать код раздела «Octave»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="C">C</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=27" title="Редактировать раздел «C»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Редактировать код раздела «C»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-cpp mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="k">typedef</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">function</span><span class="p">)(</span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">);</span>

<span class="c1">//Выбор начального приближения</span>
<span class="n">xn</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">MyFunction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">A</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">My2Derivative</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">A</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">?</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">B</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">A</span><span class="p">;</span>

<span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nf">MyFunction</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">return</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">pow</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.2</span><span class="p">);</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Ваша функция</span>
<span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nf">MyDerivative</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">return</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">pow</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">);</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Первая производная</span>
<span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nf">My2Derivative</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">return</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">20</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">pow</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">));</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">//Вторая производная</span>

<span class="c1">-- Функция solve универсальна для всех вещественных типов значения которых можно сравнивать.</span>
<span class="nf">solve</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="ow">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">esolve</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mf">0.000001</span>

<span class="nf">esolve</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">epsilon</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">func</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">deriv</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="ow">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">fst</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">.</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">head</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">$</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">dropWhile</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">pred</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">pairs</span>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="n">next</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">xn</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="ow">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">xn</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">-</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">func</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">xn</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">/</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">deriv</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">xn</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c1">-- Функция next вычисляет новое приближение.</span>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fortran"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fortran" title="Fortran">Fortran</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;veaction=edit&amp;section=29" title="Редактировать раздел «Fortran»"><span>править</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B4_%D0%9D%D1%8C%D1%8E%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD%D0%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Редактировать код раздела «Fortran»"><span>править код</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-fortran mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="c">!   Main program</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kt">REAL</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="mi">8</span><span class="kd">::</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Xbeg</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">F</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">D1F</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">error</span><span class="w">  </span><span class="c">! Имена переменных в главной программе и подпрограмме могут отличаться    </span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kt">INTEGER  </span><span class="n">Niter</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Ncalc</span><span class="w">         </span><span class="c">! Xbeg - начальное значение, F - функция, D1F - её производная, error - остаточная ошибка</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="o">***</span><span class="w">                       </span><span class="c">! Niter - заданное число итераций, Ncalc - число выполненных итераций до достижения погрешности</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">CALL </span><span class="n">NEWTON</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Xbeg</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Niter</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">F</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">D1F</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Ncalc</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">error</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="o">***</span>
<span class="n">C</span><span class="o">======================================================</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">SUBROUTINE </span><span class="n">NEWTON</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Func</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">D1Func</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nevl</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">rer</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="c">! Простейший вариант устойчиво работающей программы для нахождения корня  без второй производной                                                               </span>

<span class="w">	</span><span class="kt">REAL</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="mi">8</span><span class="kd">::</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">X1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">XB</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">q</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Func</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">D1Func</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">rer</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">eps</span><span class="w">       </span><span class="c">! Итог вычисления будет записан в переменную Х0</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="kt">INTEGER  </span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nevl</span>
<span class="w">	</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">IF</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1000</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">LE</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">1000</span><span class="w">                 </span><span class="c">! Защита от дурака</span>
<span class="w">	                </span><span class="n">Nevl</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">XB</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">X0</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">DO </span><span class="n">I</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nmax</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">IF</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">EQ</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="mf">0.</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w">            </span><span class="k">EXIT</span>
<span class="k">    IF</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">D1Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">EQ</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="mf">0.</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w">          </span><span class="k">THEN</span>
<span class="k">    Print</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">*</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">'Error from NEWTON: D1Func='</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">D1Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">),</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">'  X='</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">'  I='</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">I</span>
<span class="w">                                  </span><span class="k">EXIT</span>
<span class="k">    END IF                   </span>
<span class="k">		</span>
<span class="k">	</span><span class="n">X1</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">D1Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span>
<span class="w">	</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="n">q</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">D1Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">));</span><span class="w">  </span><span class="n">q</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mf">1.</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">q</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">/</span><span class="n">q</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="n">eps</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="nb">MAX</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rer</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nb">epsilon</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">))</span><span class="w">                           </span><span class="c">! epsilon(X0) - машинная точность; выбирается, если rer=0.</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">IF</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="n">X1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">LE</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">q</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">eps</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w">       </span><span class="k">EXIT</span>
<span class="k">	</span>
<span class="k">	</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">X1</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">END DO</span>
<span class="k">    </span>
<span class="k">    IF</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">X0</span><span class="p">)).</span><span class="n">GE</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nb">abs</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Func</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">XB</span><span class="p">)))</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">PAUSE</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s1">'Error from NEWTON: Change the X0!'</span>

<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">If</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">I</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">ne</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nevl</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">I</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">If</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">I</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">eq</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Nmax</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">Nevl</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">Nmax</span>
<span class="w">	</span>
<span class="w">	</span><span class="k">END SUBROUTINE</span>
